"><div class="wikiContents _021e collapsed ca53"><h1> <!-- -->MS in UK for Indian Students - Universities, Colleges, Fees 2023, Deadlines</h1><div class="faq__according-wrapper"><div><p><strong>Study MS in UK: </strong>The UK has an amazing history of academic excellence. It is one of the<a href="https://studyabroad.shiksha.com/why-is-the-uk-a-popular-location-for-higher-studies-articlepage-634">favourite countries for international students</a> to pursue their higher education. Especially when it comes to MS in UK universities, they are at the forefront of offering a wide range of courses based on the interest of the student. MS in UK offers full-time 1- or 2-years courses available in research, course-based, or a combination of both programmes. UK universities offer specialists with a wide range of professions, fields, and courses to choose from, allowing international students to pursue their preferred degree program. MS in Engineering, General Science, and Computer Science are some of the most sought-after MS courses for students who want to pursue them abroad.</p>

<h2 class="setSide">Cost of studying MS in UK</h2> 
<p>This section will brief you about the average cost of studying MS in UK and the cost of living in UK for international students. The average first-year cost of studying MS in UK is INR 21.41 lakhs. The average cost of living in UK is around INR12.12 lakhs per year.</p> 
<h3>Student Visa Cost for UK</h3> 
<ul> 
 <li>Fee for a Student visa while applying from outside the UK: 363</li> 
 <li>Fee for extension or switching to a Student visa from inside UK: 490</li> 
</ul> 
<p><strong>Check:<a href="https://studyabroad.shiksha.com/when-to-start-thinking-about-finances-to-study-abroad-articlepage-1471">When to start thinking about Finances to Study Abroad</a></strong></p> 
<h2>MS requirements for UK  Eligibility Criteria</h2> 
<p>Candidates looking to pursue MS in UK are required to fulfil these primary requirements:</p> 
<ol> 
 <li>Candidate must have 3 to 4 years of graduation degree in a related field</li> 
 <li>Most universities require GMAT/GRE scores for admission</li> 
 <li>For pursuing MS in the UK, students must appear in English proficiency tests such as IELTS, TOFEL, and PTE; followed by a personal interview conducted by some universities.</li> 
 <li>Minimum of 2 years of work experience for getting enrolled in UK universities. However, its not always mandatory.</li> 
</ol> 
<h2>Work Permit after studying MS in UK</h2> 
<p>The UK Post-Student Work visa allows international students to stay in UK to seek work for a period of 2 years after completing their studies. The rule applies to bachelor's, masters and Ph.D. graduates. Make sure you're in the UK when applying for the same. The permit will last three years if you're pursuing a PhD or any other doctoral degree. Please note that extending your graduate visa is not possible and you can switch to a skilled worker visa or another instead of that.</p> 
<p>Graduate Visa Costs</p> 
<ul style="list-style-type: undefined;"> 
 <li>Application fee: 715</li> 
 <li>Healthcare Surcharge: 624 each year</li> 
</ul> 
<p><strong>Check:<a href="https://studyabroad.shiksha.com/post-study-work-permit-in-uk-applycontent5977">Post Study Work Permit in UK (PSW UK): About Graduate Route</a></strong></p>

<p>International MS students in UK can apply for many scholarships. Candidates seeking MS scholarships to study in UK can view the most comprehensive study of abroad scholarships mentioned on our website. Our website currently registers more than 200 scholarships distributed across 11 countries.</p>

<h2>MS in UK FAQs</h2> 
<p><strong>Q. How much does MS in UK cost?</strong></p> 
<p>A. The average first-year cost of studying MS in UK is INR 21.41 lakhs. The average cost of living in UK is around INR 12.12 lakhs per year.OverseasMS students in UK can apply for many scholarships to fund their studies. Candidates seeking MS scholarships to study in UK can view the most comprehensive study of abroad scholarships mentioned on our website.</p> 
<p><strong>Q. What is the duration of MS in UK?</strong></p> 
<p>A. MS in UK offers full-time 1- or 2-years courses available in research, course-based, or a combination of both programs.MS in Engineering, General Science, and Computer Science are some of the most sought-after MS courses for students who want to pursue them abroad.</p> 
<p><strong>Q. Is GRE required for MS in UK?</strong></p> 
<p>A. UK does not require GRE points in its MS programs.</p> 
<p><strong>Q. Are there scholarships to study MS in UK?</strong></p> 
<p>A. Yes, you can check a comprehensive list of a variety of scholarships that you can apply for on our website.</p> 
<p><strong>Q. What are the top scholarships for candidates who want to pursue MS in UK?</strong></p> 
<p>A. Some of the scholarships for candidates who want to pursue MS in UK are:</p> 
<ul> 
 <li>Narotam Sekhsarias Scholarships</li> 
 <li>Hani Zeini Scholarship</li> 
 <li>Harvey Fellowship</li> 
 <li>Inlaks Scholarships (University Courses)</li> 
 <li>Global Study Awards</li> 
 <li>Erasmus Mundus Joint Masters scholarships</li>

function showShikshaAssistant(){
  if(window.assistantInit === true){
    return;
  }
  
  
  if(!(document.getElementById("chat-container") == null)){
    window.assistantInit = true;
    var d = new Date();
    var imported = document.createElement('script');
    imported.src = 'https://js.shiksha.ws/public/js/chatplugin.js?'+d.getDate()+''+(d.getMonth()+1)+''+d.getFullYear()+'3';
    imported.async = 1;
    // imported.defer = 1;
    document.head.appendChild(imported);
  }
}

  showShikshaAssistant(); 
}

function closeBanner1(){
  if(document.getElementById('stickyBanner')){
    document.getElementById("stickyBanner").style.display = "none";
    var element = document.getElementById('tocCapsule'); // To move Toc if ABanner is closed
    if(element && element.classList && element.classList.add && element.setAttribute) {
      element.setAttribute('data-closed', true);
      element.classList.add("closed");
    } 
  }
}

  }
}

function loadMultipleCSS(cssArrayList){
  if(cssArrayList && cssArrayList.length>0){
    cssArrayList.forEach(function(url) {
      var script = document.createElement('link');
      script.href = url;
      script.rel = 'stylesheet';
      script.type = 'text/css';
      document.body.appendChild(script);
    });
  }
}

function loadMultipleScriptOneByOne(scriptArayList){
  return new Promise( function( resolve, reject ) {
    var listItem = scriptArayList.shift();
    if(listItem){
      var s = document.createElement('script');
      var r = false;
      s.type = 'text/javascript';
      s.src = listItem;
      s.async = true;
      s.onerror = function(err) {
        if(scriptArayList.length > 0 ) {      
          loadMultipleScriptOneByOne(scriptArayList).then( function() {
              resolve();
          });
        } else {
          reject(err, s);
        }
      };
      s.onload = s.onreadystatechange = function() {
        // console.log(this.readyState); // uncomment this line to see which ready states are called.
        if (!r && (!this.readyState || this.readyState == 'complete')) {
          r = true;
          if(scriptArayList.length > 0 ) {      
            loadMultipleScriptOneByOne(scriptArayList).then( function() {
                resolve();
            });
          } else {
              resolve();
          }
        }
      };
      var t = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
      t.parentElement.insertBefore(s, t);    
    }else{
      resolve();
    }
  });
}
function openChatBotRegistration(paramsObject,callBackFunction,onClose){
  //versioning the files
  var eVr=new Date();
  var tVr= eVr.getDate()+""+eVr.getMonth()+eVr.getFullYear()+"9";
  var cssArray = ['https://js.shiksha.ws/public/css/convMMP.css?v='+tVr];
  var jsArray = ['https://js.shiksha.ws/public/js/jquery-3.5.1.min.js?v='+tVr,'https://js.shiksha.ws/public/js/vue.js?v='+tVr,'https://js.shiksha.ws/public/js/chatui.js?v='+tVr,'https://js.shiksha.ws/public/js/convMMP.js?v='+tVr];
  if(typeof(paramsObject) == 'object' && paramsObject.entityId > 0){
    if(typeof(loadConversationalMMP) === 'function'){
      loadConversationalMMP(paramsObject,callBackFunction,onClose);
    }else{
      loadMultipleCSS(cssArray);
      loadMultipleScriptOneByOne(jsArray).then(function (res) {
        loadConversationalMMP(paramsObject,callBackFunction,onClose);
      })
    }  
  }  
  
}
